Details of the Counterfeit Money Case Cracked in Qingdao

▲ Japanese Counterfeiting Organizations Had Three Locations in Qingdao

▲ Over the Past Five Years, They Have Sold 2 Million Yuan Worth of Counterfeit Money

▲ Nine Principal Offenders Have Been Arrested in Various Locations

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao Public Security Bureau cracked a major case last month involving the Japanese Yamazaki Tomisaburo (alias Chou Tian Jizhi Zhu), who was counterfeiting banknotes. The details of the crackdown are recorded as follows:

▲ Printing Organizations After Yamazaki Tomisaburo, who was using the alias "Chou Tian Jizhi Zhu," was arrested by the Public Security Bureau, and because the sellers of counterfeit money, Yin Songshan, Sun Rubin, and others, provided evidence, Yamazaki could not deny it and had to confess the truth. All the printing locations were provided by the offender, totaling three places: one at No. 60 Guanxian Road, one at a Russian residence on Hunan Road, and one behind the Dakang Yarn Factory in Dongzhen. According to his confession, all the counterfeit money was printed through eighteen overprinting plates, so it was manufactured in three places to avoid attracting attention. The chief printing technician was Nishijima Misaku, who used to run a printing shop in Tokyo, Japan, and was very skilled in printing technology. The authenticity of the printed banknotes was difficult to distinguish at a glance. Nishijima and Fujimoto were both old friends. In 1926, they invited him to Qingdao to serve as a printing technician. The Japanese Consulate has arrested Nishijima and, together with Yamazaki, is holding him in custody at the Japanese Consulate.

▲ Principal Offenders Arrested The discovery of this counterfeit money dates back to 1926. At that time, it was only known that there was this counterfeit money on the market, and it was known that it was made by the Japanese, but it was not yet expected that its manufacturing organization was nesting among the Japanese residents of Qingdao, who were shielded by consular jurisdiction. This matter originated with Fujisaki Caijiro, Hashimoto Susumu, Tsujita Harujiro, and others taking the initiative. At that time, after they invited the printing technician Nishijima to Qingdao, they organized step by step. Yamazaki Tomisaburo took on the job of sales. Over the years, they have sold 2 million yuan worth of counterfeit money along the Jiaoji Railway and in the Shanghai area. After this case occurred, Fujisaki Caijiro and Hashimoto Susumu both fled to Shanghai, and Tsujita Genjiro fled back to Kyoto, Japan. The Japanese Consulate has stated that Fujisaki and Hashimoto have been arrested in Shanghai, and Tsujita Genjiro has also been arrested in Kyoto and will be brought to justice. In addition, Yoshida Goro, Yamamoto Keishiro, Niimi Ryuichi, and others residing in this city are all important offenders in this case. They are currently being detained and held in custody by the Japanese Consulate.

▲ Seized Stolen Goods After this case was cracked, more than forty types of printing machines, more than 16,000 counterfeit ten-yuan banknotes, and thousands of counterfeit five-yuan and one-yuan banknotes were seized from the counterfeit printing organizations and the residences of the offenders. It can be seen that the Japanese and others were very well-organized. The counterfeit money they printed was not only the ten-yuan type, but also the five-yuan and one-yuan types were printed together to facilitate sales. This matter has a great impact on China's finances. Our banking industry must not take this case lightly. They should unite and petition the government to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese ambassador. Because this counterfeit money is scattered everywhere, society is harmed by it, and the banking industry is even more affected. (March 2nd)

Trial of the Communist Party Case in Tianjin Concluded

▲ Yu Xuezhong Has Telegraphed Zhang for Instructions

Beiping Correspondence: On the evening of the 10th of last month, Zhang Xueming, Director of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau, and Liu Butong, member of the Reorganization Committee, arrested Han Qingfu, Chairman of the Special Committee of the Communist Party in the Rehe-Chahar-Suiyuan Special Districts, and Zheng Pilie, Chairman of the Military Committee of the Communist Party in the Northern District, and thirty-seven others at the Yuzhong Hotel in the French Concession. On the 16th, they were escorted to Beiping and sent by the Beiping Public Security Bureau to the Pingjin Garrison Headquarters. Commander Yu Xuezhong, considering the seriousness of the case, personally interrogated them for several days. By the 23rd, the entire case had been interrogated. On the 24th, the entire case was telegraphed to Deputy Commander Zhang for instructions. According to those who participated in this interrogation, Han Qingfu and Zheng Pilie were the main figures among the more than thirty people arrested. Han was originally an extremely poor student. After graduating from Peking University, he joined various activities that disrupted social order. In his childhood, he used to sell opium. Later, he joined the Communist Party. In 1924, when the Kuomintang was reorganized, he also joined the Kuomintang. He often used the pretext of luring one or two Mongols, claiming to be Mongolian revolutionary comrades, and swindled large sums of money from Kuomintang figures, using part of it for his personal extravagance and the rest as funding for Communist Party activities. In other words, Han was nominally a member of the Kuomintang, but secretly swindled money from the Kuomintang and worked for the Communist Party. After the Kuomintang's purge of the Communists in 1927, his nomination as a candidate for the Central Executive Committee was revoked. For a time, he joined the Third Party, but later betrayed the Third Party. When he arrived in Tianjin, he still worked for the Third Party. In 1928, when Zhang Zongchang was defeated and retreated to eastern Tianjin, Han, under the name of a Communist commander, collected many refugees and kidnapped the president of the Chamber of Commerce in Yahuangqiao Town, extorting thousands of dollars. Recently, he was extremely bored in Tianjin. It happened that a certain route commander sent his advisor, Du, to Tianjin to purchase weapons. Du was a Communist Party member and a fellow villager with Han. Han then instigated Du to abscond with 250,000 yuan for weapons, allocating part of it for private sharing and the rest as a working fund, recruiting refugees, and establishing his own banner outside the orthodox Communist Party. He used part of the embezzled funds to assign his younger brother, Han Zhizhong, to transport and sell opium in Chifeng, Chaoyang, Jinzhou, and Liaoning. He used another part of the funds to open a car dealership, traveling between Chifeng and Beipiao, ostensibly to transport passengers, but in reality, the purpose was to transport military supplies and support bandits. He also gave a portion of the funds to his relative, Lu Xiangxuan, for high-interest loans. All the remaining profits from selling opium, transporting military supplies, and lending at high interest were used as Han's party working expenses. His work plan was to use Beipiao as a base camp, because there were coal mines in the area, and all the miners were organized by Han into a group, waiting for the opportunity to act. He also colluded with Ma Hongtu and Zhang Chaobin, employees of the Chaoyang Temple Railway Station, and local bandit leaders Li Xiangxuan and Yao Guangxin, among others, to commit kidnapping and robbery in order to collect money. Han proclaimed himself the Zhu De and Mao Zedong of the Northwest and had long planned to take the opportunity to riot, first launching a guerrilla war in Rehe, and then expanding to the northern provinces. Han's ambitions were very great. Last spring, he sent Guo Gaoxuan's wife to Kulun to win over the Communist Party of Outer Mongolia and the Red Russians, planning to integrate all the areas outside the Great Wall with Russia and Mongolia, and then rise up. It is said that Guo's trip has achieved considerable success, but Russia and Mongolia regard Han as an undisciplined member outside the organization of the Chinese Communist Party, so they have not provided substantial assistance. Recently, since Han obtained funds from a certain commander, he recruited troops and horses, and his power has grown. The Communist Party then restored Han's party membership and appointed him as the chairman of the Special Committee of the three districts of Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan, to show their support. Zheng Pilie was Han's right-hand man, skilled in riding and shooting. All the killings committed by Han's party were done by Zheng. Han initiated the assassination of Wang Zaowen and Li Lanting, Tianjin Communist Party members, in 1928, and Zheng personally fired the shots. Recently, the robbery of a train on the Jin-Chao branch line of the Beiping-Liaoning Railway was also rumored to be related to Han and Zheng. The planning and strategies all came from these people. The bandits who fired the shots were only their pawns. The Rehe natives in Beiping believe that Han's actions are enough to endanger the stability and order of Rehe, and they have jointly petitioned Deputy Commander Zhang to severely punish him in order to eradicate the roots of communism (March 1st). Songjiang

Xiahengjing Robbery Case Quickly Solved Xiahengjing Town in Punan is a small market town about six li from Tinglin. The previous night (the 2nd), more than twenty bandits suddenly came to the town and searched and robbed all the larger stores before fleeing. Someone followed them and saw the bandits carrying their loot enter a certain village not far away. Knowing their whereabouts, they returned to report to the First Branch of the Tinglin Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to guide them in the search and arrest. Eight people were captured and taken back for investigation. Further arrests and research are pending.

Discussing Methods for Suppressing Bandits The banditry in Punan, within the borders of Songjiang and Jinshan counties, is currently being suppressed on a large scale. At a joint suppression meeting of Songjiang and Jinshan counties the other day, it was decided that all teahouse owners must sign a pledge with the district office. Those who do not comply will be sealed up by the county upon presentation by the district. The county government is responsible for ordering the public security bureaus to seal all opium dens by March 15th. These measures have been implemented separately. In addition, because local hidden spies are often afraid of the bandits' fierceness and fear retaliation, they dare not report them, which is a major obstacle to the suppression effort. The county government has specially instructed the district chiefs of the 12th District (Tinglin), 15th District (Caojing), and 16th District (Shanyang) to set up confidential report boxes and report the establishment and management methods before March 15th. The Construction Bureau is also ordered to expedite the installation of long-distance telephones within the above three districts in order to ensure timely communication.

Fang Baolong Kidnapping Case Bandits Demand Ransom a Second Time Fang Baolong, a resident of Si'an Township, Xiaojing Township, in the 11th District of this county, and his grandson were kidnapped by bandits on January 26. Lu Shiqiao Reactionary Case Opens Another Hearing Lu Shiqiao, a doctor from Beishang Township, Wuxi, and Lu Genhu, Guo Asi, Zhu A'da, and others were sentenced to imprisonment by the High Court for joining the Communist Party. The appeal case of Lu Shiqiao's murder case is scheduled to be heard on the 23rd of this month.

One was wearing a black serge long gown, and the other two were wearing short blue cloth uniforms, resembling workers. They carried a pistol and declared that they wanted to borrow 500 yuan. Changshu

Hupu Public Security Bureau Chief Investigated for Embezzlement of Opium On July 28th of last year, the Sixth Branch of the Hupu Public Security Bureau received a report that the Jin Changyu seagoing ship was importing and smuggling opium. Shao Gengsheng, the director of the bureau, led several officers to inspect the ship. As a result, eleven packages of opium were seized and sent to the county. Later, a citizen named Shen Mumu filed a complaint with the county and the Central Anti-Opium Commission, alleging that Director Shao had seized 132.5 pounds of opium, which did not match the amount sent, and that he had obviously embezzled some of it. The Anti-Opium Commission ordered the Civil Affairs Department to transfer the case to the county for investigation. The county sent personnel to the countryside three times to investigate, but the investigation was not thorough. As a result, the Public Security Bureau Director Shao Gengsheng was only given a demerit as a formality. The Civil Affairs Department, after being informed, believed that since it was a case of embezzlement of opium, a demerit was not enough. They instructed the county to investigate further. The county government, after receiving the order, questioned the plaintiff and defendant on January 29th in the administrative section of the county government. The 2nd of this month was the date for the second round of questioning. This time, the defendant, the boatman Chen San, the director of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Shao Gengsheng, the plaintiff, Shen Mumu, and the witness, Hu Sheng, the district chief of the 15th District, were all subpoenaed. All except the witness reported on that day. At 2:00 p.m., the examining judge, Gu, opened the court for questioning. First, the defendant, Chen San, was questioned. He testified that he used to be a crew member and is now doing small business. At that time, a fellow crew member reported me for smuggling 2.5 pounds of opium. I was very shocked because Zhu Zhenhuan himself loaded opium in Dalian and brought it back, but instead reported me. So I told them what they said, and Director Shao came to investigate and take it away, totaling eleven packages. Next, the plaintiff, Shen Mumu, was questioned. She testified that when the opium was inspected, I went to see it myself. A sack, a bamboo basket, and a bamboo container were found at the boat wharf behind the district office. In addition, someone was holding 2.5 pounds. If it was not 132.5 pounds, then it was definitely more than eleven packages. There was obvious embezzlement, and there were several suspicious points: (1) Inspecting opium on a ship is within the scope of the water police. Why didn't Director Shao go with the water police to inspect the opium? (2) After it was seized, it was taken to the bureau. District Chief Hu Sheng requested to seal it together, but Shao refused. (3) In this case, the boatman Chen San was dismissed by the shipowner after the incident. Chen had nowhere to go, so Director Shao took him in and appointed him as an inspector. (4) Shao had rendered meritorious service by seizing the opium, so why was he given a demerit by the county government? (5) Shao is a dignified director, and I am a commoner. If it is not true, why doesn't he sue me for false accusation? All of the above are inexplicable questions. I have no feud with him. However, according to Dr. Sun Yat-sen's instructions, opium harms society. If anyone conquers opium, he is a public enemy of the people. That is why I stood up to report it. Finally, the defendant, Shao Gengsheng, the director of the Hupu Public Security Bureau, was questioned. He testified that someone reported on July 28th of last year that there was opium on the ship, so I went to inspect it. I opened it with an axe in the partition under the stove and found nine packages, plus two packages in the basket, totaling eleven packages, which were all sent to the county. There was no embezzlement. As for District Chief Hu and Assistant Ren Fei'an, they never came to seal it together, otherwise how could I have refused him? Chen San was also not appointed as an inspector, and the branch bureau does not have this authority, and even the general bureau does not have this title. These are all his words. Please investigate. As a result, the official instructed Shen Mumu to provide a guarantee. Shen said, "If it is not true, just nail me up and put me in prison," and then added a seal and retired. Then, it was ordered to summon the witnesses Hu Sheng and Ren Fei'an for a second hearing. The court adjourned immediately.

Wuxi

Defendant in Murder Case Files an Appeal Guo Zizhen, a resident of Dai Lane near Meirong Mountain in the Sixth District of this county (i.e., Tianxia City), was beaten to death by villagers two years ago. His wife, Mao, filed a petition with the county government to investigate. More than ten people were arrested. Those who were found to be irrelevant after interrogation by the county government were released on bail. However, Zhang Apan, Ni Apei, Ni Rongpei, Dai Chaosheng, and several others were sentenced to four, five, or eight years of imprisonment by the county. Recently, the county court was established, and the county government transferred the case files to the court. Zhang Apan and others were not satisfied with the county judgment and filed an appeal with the High Court. Yesterday, the court sent bailiffs to escort Zhang Apan and others to the High Court for questioning and verification.

County Public Security Bureau's Crackdown on Gambling Causes an Uproar Lu Tianfu, who runs a small teahouse in Daxuankou in the Fourth District, has been opening gambling dens in the countryside for days. Someone came to the city to report to the Supervision Office of the County Public Security Bureau, which dispatched Patrol Chief Chen to lead a squad of police to the scene. They found more than ten gamblers gambling inside and planned to arrest them. The gamblers immediately caused an uproar. Patrol Chief Chen immediately reported to the Ninth Branch of the District Security Bureau and the County Public Security Bureau, which dispatched police to the scene one after another. All the gamblers had already escaped. The owner, Lu Tianfu, was arrested and sent to the city for verification. Sixty-Year-Old Man Drowns Himself Liu Wenlan, a resident of this county, was over sixty years old. He used to work for the Beitang Miscellaneous Goods Guild and is now retired at home. Due to economic pressure, he drowned himself under the Xinqiao Bridge inside the Guangfu Gate at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. He was spotted by someone, who pulled Liu out of the water and sent him to the Labor Hospital for treatment, but he died. His son, Da Bao, arrived at the scene to claim the body.

Those that have been investigated but not yet scheduled for a joint accounting should be urged to schedule a joint accounting as soon as possible, or to conduct a joint monitoring and accounting, to conduct a fair accounting, and to submit a register for reporting. According to the investigation, the unfinished handovers of Jiangyin include the seven terms of the former magistrates Zhang Zongyi, Huang Yuzao, Wang Jiajin, Wu Peng, Liu Shou, Zeng Wangzuo, and Shen Bingyan. Except for the five terms of Zhang, Huang, Wu, Liu, and Shen, which have been registered and accounted for, the remaining two terms of Wang Jiajin and Wang Guozuo have also been registered and submitted long ago. Director Shen has repeatedly urged the two former magistrates to come to Cheng as soon as possible for a joint accounting, but there has been no response. The Department of Finance has approved the separate transfer of instructions to the native provinces and local authorities of the two former magistrates, ordering them to come to Cheng for a joint accounting. If there is still no response, the situation will be reported in accordance with the fourth item of the Measures, together with the monitoring and accounting. Letter from Shen Xun Chu of Zhujiajiao

To the esteemed editor: Having read the Qingpu correspondence in the Huang Bao on March 2nd, the section regarding the manager of Changyuan Farm in Zhujiajiao does not accord with the facts. Changyuan was established in the spring of the 18th year [of the Republic] when Xun Chu invited shareholders from Qingjiao to participate. After two years of operation, the profits totaled 12,000 yuan. A shareholders meeting was convened on February 19th of this year to announce the dissolution. All farm affairs have been inspected and handed over to the shareholders. As for Xun Chu's personal debts, they have been forgiven by the shareholders. I have never left Zhujiajiao during the farm's operations. How could I have absconded with the funds and abandoned my family? This matter concerns my reputation and should be corrected. Sincerely, Shen Xun Chu, former Manager of Changyuan Farm in Zhujiajiao, March 4th.

He Jian Consults the Ministry of Education on Improving School Curricula

▲Select and Diligently Teach the Maxims of Chinese and Foreign Philosophers

▲Select Individuals of Excellent Scholarship and Conduct to Manage Education

Changsha Communication, February 24th. He Jian, Chairman of the Provincial Government, has repeatedly consulted the Ministry of Education, in addition to pointing out the shortcomings of education and requesting improvements. Yesterday, he again acted upon the detailed report of the Dong'an County Magistrate, requesting improvements to school curricula. He believes that improving textbooks is the most urgent task at present and has consulted the Ministry of Education for verification and action. The original consultation is appended below.

Regarding the matter of consultation: According to a statement by former Dong'an County Magistrate Tang Zhengyi, entitled "Improving School Curricula": Schools have been established for more than twenty years, but the majority of those who set up Communist organizations in the past were students, and the majority of those who joined the Communist Party's battle groups this time were also students. The effects of exhausting public and private resources to train these troublemakers are evident. Before the eighth year [of the Republic], the Chinese textbooks in various schools still had literary merit. Recently, the textbooks have been filled with dog-speak, pig-speak, duck-speak, and terms like "Miss Cat," "Elder Brother Dog," and "Old Man Ox," filling the lines. Animals can speak human language, honorifics are applied to animals, and the language is vulgar and bizarre beyond description. There is also a kind of absurd statement (such as "Dad, you help people build houses every day, but you don't have a house yourself"), and (phrases like "My fist is big, my arms are thick"), which are tantamount to promoting communism and inciting violence. Young people's character is not yet firm, and they are often confused by this. If such books are distributed in schools and listed as curricula, it is tantamount to eliminating visible Communists on one hand and creating a large number of invisible Communists on the other. Even if one speaks of eliminating the Communists daily, what benefit is there? Now heresies are rampant, and bandits are growing daily. Fortunately, there are still Confucian scholars in the wilderness who revere morality, and there are still generals in the country who uphold justice, who can contend in the realm of entering people and entering beasts, forming this half-governed, half-chaotic situation. If another few decades pass, humanity will perish, and all will be able to lead beasts to devour people, and people will devour each other. The massacres of Huang Chao, Li Zicheng, and Zhang Xianzhong will not be difficult to see again. I fear that there will be immeasurable and boundless catastrophes. For the present plan, all school textbooks that are difficult and inappropriate, and those with shallow theories that are not practical, should be burned. It is especially appropriate to select and diligently teach the maxims of Chinese and foreign philosophers, and it is necessary to select those with both excellent scholarship and conduct to manage education. This is also a method of dredging rivers to suppress floods and holding fire to drive away fierce beasts. The钧座 [honorific title] issued a telegram in the past year regarding carefully selecting teachers. If the previous proposal is brought up again and implemented, then the merit will be immortal. The house is collapsing, and what is pressed will be destroyed. The rhinoceros horn is not far away, and deep concern is felt. I offer my humble opinion for consideration. Is it appropriate? Please examine it, etc. The review of textbooks is the most urgent task at present. Based on the reasons stated earlier, in addition to the reply, a corresponding consultation is submitted to your department, requesting that it be verified and handled, and hoping to see a reply. This consultation.

Jinan City Education Administrative Conference

A Jinan express dispatch states that the Jinan City Education Bureau held the opening ceremony of the Municipal School Education Administrative Conference at the bureau at 8:00 AM today (the 1st). In addition to the bureau director, secretary, section chiefs, inspectors, and directors, the principals of all municipal elementary schools and the directors of various public schools all participated, totaling more than thirty people. The conference was chaired by Zhang Hongjian, Director of the bureau, with Zhang Anzhi as the master of ceremonies and Zhao Zhonglu as the recorder. After the ceremony, the chairman gave the opening speech, roughly stating: "Distinguished principals, distinguished directors, today's first administrative conference of municipal schools is of profound significance and extremely important mission. I will explain it in six points: 1. The Education Bureau has only been established for three months. Although there is an overall plan for how to improve and popularize education in Jinan, the plan may not be thorough due to limited talent and resources. I hope that you will gather together to discuss and assist in the implementation. 2. The highest principle of current education is the Three Principles of the People. How can we make the students and teachers' thoughts converge on the Three Principles of the People? I hope that you will discuss this in detail and formulate the moral education standards and implementation plans for each school based on the Three Principles of the People, in order to realize the Party-based education. 3. We know that under the same circumstances, the quality of teaching methods varies, and the educational efficiency obtained is vastly different. I hope that everyone will base their daily teaching experience and discuss the improvement of teaching methods in detail at this conference. 4. The city's schools are divided into provincial, municipal, and private. Provincial schools have more generous funding, private schools often worry about insufficient funding, and municipal schools have less funding than provincial schools, but are still more numerous than private schools. I hope you will work hard and strive for progress, so as not to fall behind. 5. The budget preparation for the 19th year [of the Republic] may not be suitable in some places. I hope everyone will deliberate and discuss and stipulate the standards for budget distribution in order to prepare the budget for the 20th year. 6. The current funding for each school is relatively difficult. Under these strained circumstances, we should break through the economic difficulties and strive to obtain the greatest effect with the smallest consumption, so that education will have new development. Furthermore, education is divided into social education and school education. School education cultivates talents, which is certainly important, but social education has the function of changing customs and habits and should also be given equal importance. In short, to run education in Jinan City, we must ensure that there are no dropouts in the urban area and that no citizen is illiterate, so that education will be considered a success. But education is a social undertaking, and it cannot be popularized by the efforts of a few people. I especially hope that the citizens of Jinan and the education authorities will work together to seek development," etc. Afterwards, elementary school principals Kong Manqing, Zhou Kejun, Xia Yuzhi, etc., spoke successively. Then Xia Yuxuan was elected as vice chairman, and Wang Guanchen and Zhou Kejun were elected as secretaries. Then the photo was taken and the meeting adjourned. The general meeting continued at 2:00 PM and adjourned until 6:00 PM.

Local News

Chinese Medical Association Petitions the Central Government to Revise the Medical Education System

The Chinese Medical Association yesterday submitted a petition to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Executive and Legislative Yuan, advocating that medical education should still adopt the two-tier system in order to be practical. The original petition stated: "The petition is to earnestly request the revision of the medical education system and the restoration of specialized medical schools in order to cultivate daily-use talents and benefit health construction. The establishment of scientific medical education in our country began at the end of the Qing Dynasty. Students were sent to study medicine abroad, and after returning to the country, they united with comrades to establish specialized medical schools in various provinces and cities. For more than ten years, although not many talents have been cultivated, they have opened clinics and established hospitals in major ports to relieve suffering, barely supporting the facade. During the Northern Expedition, tens of thousands of people were killed or injured in years of war. The medical assistance and subsequent treatment provided by these people for field operations was invaluable. Therefore, if our country wants to seek the universality of medicine among the people and the progress of health administration, it should pay attention to improving the quality and, more importantly, increasing the quantity. This is an immutable conclusion. However, in the 17th year [of the Republic], the education authorities forgot the transition and, in the name of vigorously implementing elite medical education, wanted to implement their policy of moving mountains and exceeding seas. They changed the school system and either ordered the immediate closure of specialized medical schools in various provinces that had achieved success, or limited the period for their completion. The number of medical colleges that they advocated was small and the number of students was countable. Except for the Peking and Guangzhou colleges, which replaced the old equipment of the specialized medical schools with a university signboard, the only one that was painstakingly operated was the Wusong Central University Medical College produced by Jiangsu Medical University. The total number of students, combined for all four grades, is less than one hundred. Together with the Peking and Guangzhou colleges, the total number of medical talents graduating each year is less than one hundred and fifty, causing society to sigh for the lack of doctors and youth to cut off people's access to medicine. This is nothing more than the natural and inevitable result of the current situation of lacking both money and talent, and pursuing vain fame. Men of insight in the medical field are worried about it. Therefore, at the first Central Health Conference in the 18th year [of the Republic], two resolutions, numbered 中字第十 and 十二十三, were passed. The main point is to restore the two-tier system in order to train practical talents for the future. The Medical Education System Committee of the former University Council also agreed in the first article of the general outline when formulating the medical school system, which stated that "this standard is divided into two types: specialized medicine and medical colleges or medical universities." Because medical experts are more concerned and know more details, after several careful considerations, everyone agreed that the two-tier system is the urgent need and must be restored. However, the former education authorities, under pressure from public opinion, were able to add an article on setting up a specialized medical department within the university regulations. However, the existing specialized medical schools were limited to closing in stages and were not allowed to exist independently. As a result, the principals of the specialized medical schools in Baoding, Nanchang, Hangzhou, and other places were busy traveling back and forth to the capital for consultations, but no agreement was reached. Some teachers and students were eagerly campaigning to protect the schools, running around calling for help, but without effect. Medical education was precarious, and the impact was that science lagged behind. This was all caused by the former education authorities' ignorance of the needs of the times and their adherence to outdated prejudices. Upon investigation, what is the difference between the equipment standards and professor qualifications of the future medical department attached to the medical college envisioned by the Ministry of Education and the existing specialized medical schools in various provinces? It is nothing more than being confined to narrow interests and engaging in empty talk. I, along with my colleagues, have some knowledge of medical education, and I have repeatedly failed to understand it. If we look at the reality, it is nothing more than destroying what has been accomplished and suspending what is planned. Overturning the rain and clouds is nothing more than the strategy of the monkey-raiser to give three in the morning and four in the evening, and the loss of national economy and talent is already immeasurable. How can this be tolerated? Therefore, I sincerely ask your department to cherish money and talent, measure the national conditions, and imitate the old method of controlling feudalism to create medical talent to help the emergency. Please ask the Ministry of Education to revise the medical education system and allow the restoration of specialized medical schools, so as to cultivate practical talents widely and promote health construction. Please consider and implement it, for the public convenience."

Boy Scout Party Ideology Speech Contest

The Shanghai Council of the Chinese Boy Scouts, in order to encourage Boy Scouts throughout the city to study Party ideology and train their ability to express it, has specially scheduled a Party Ideology Speech Contest for Shanghai Boy Scouts on March 12th. Those with better results in each Boy Scout group and individually will be given prizes separately to encourage them. The competition rules are listed below.

▲Competition Rules (1) The Shanghai Council of the Chinese Boy Scouts is holding a Party Ideology Speech Contest to encourage Party Ideology research among Boy Scouts throughout the city and to train their ability to express it. (2) All registered Boy Scout troops in the city can select Boy Scout representatives to register and participate. (3) The topic of the speech competition can be self-selected, but it must not go beyond the scope of the Party Ideology. (4) The unit of participation in the competition is the troop, but because the level of Boy Scouts in each troop is uneven, it is specially divided into three groups, A, B, and C, as follows: Group A: All those with high school education or those who are currently students in coaching training schools; Group B: All those with junior high school education; Group C: All those with elementary school education. If each troop has the qualifications for two or more groups, it can also register to participate in the competition for two or more groups. (5) Each troop's speech representative can be generated by holding a preliminary round in the troop according to the Boy Scout's level, or the troop leader can directly select the best to participate. (6) The schedule for the speech competition is stipulated as follows: February 24th, each troop starts preparation; Starting March 5th, register with the council until the 7th; March 12th, hold the competition. (7) Winners of the competition, whether individual or group, will be rewarded. (8) The speech time is stipulated as follows: Group A shall not exceed ten minutes, Group B shall not exceed seven minutes, and Group C shall not exceed five minutes. (9) The competition location will be announced by the council two days before the competition. (10) These rules will be promulgated and implemented by the Shanghai Council.

▲Judgment Method (1) The judging committee will consist of seven people, appointed by the association from the following candidates: one person from the Municipal Training Department, one person from the Municipal Education Bureau, three people from the Boy Scout community, and two members of the association. (2) The judging items are divided into three types: meaning, tone, and gesture. The scoring standards are as follows: meaning accounts for 40%, tone accounts for 30%, and posture accounts for 30%. (3) The grades are listed as follows: 90 points or above is superior, 80 points or above is grade A, 60 points or above is grade B, and below 60 points is grade C. (4) After the competition, the judges will fill in the scores into the scoring table. If there is any doubt about the overall grade, it will be decided by consultation.

County Public Education Propaganda Troupe Held a Gala Yesterday

▲More Than 3,000 People Participated

▲Makeup School Held an Opening Ceremony

The Public Education Propaganda Troupe, organized by the Shanghai County Public Education Hall, the Convenient Public Education Hall, the County Farmers Education Hall, the County Library, etc., has been rotating to promote various situations in disguise since the previous day, as described in this newspaper. It is reported that the first day was in Maqiao, the second day was in Zhuanqiao, and the third day was in Minhang. Every morning, the team split up and went to various villages to carry out propaganda and speeches. The methods included disguised speeches and ordinary speeches. The speech materials included promoting cooperation, improving agriculture and horticulture, and promoting family hygiene. Farmers in each village listened attentively. The performance programs included various disguised speeches to promote livelihood, health, and family affairs education. The mobile school, piloted by the County Public Education Hall in Zigang Township, District 1, has been in operation for more than a month. Labor University's School of Social Sciences Emphasizes Physical Labor

The School of Social Sciences of the National Labor University has always had a physical labor course. In the past, due to improper allocation of working hours, it hindered students' studies. The school's students are now responsible for typesetting and printing the lecture notes required by the students in order to achieve practical results. Shandong to Survey and Determine North China Sports Field

▲ Expanding the Public Sports Field

Jinan Newsletter: The 15th North China Games track and field events and baseball and tennis teams will be held in Jinan. The Provincial 15th North China Games Preparatory Committee considered that the old site of the Provincial Public Sports Field was insufficient for use, and decided to expand and renovate it. The Department of Construction, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, and the Sports Field jointly surveyed the area. Details have been provided in previous correspondence. The survey has now been completed, and the design drawings will be made as soon as the valuation is completed and construction can begin. The original site of the sports field was 54 mu, and 11 mu have been newly purchased, for a total of 65 mu. The current design includes six tennis courts, four team ball courts, and an extended straight track to reduce the angle of the 400-meter track. The total area measures 295 meters long on the east side, 198 meters long on the west side, 180.5 meters long on the south side, and 167 meters long on the north side. A drainage ditch will be built around the entire field. The straight track will be 240 meters long and 12 meters wide. The silk ball court and team ball court will be located next to the east side of the field. The track and field area will include a football field and a baseball field. The baseball game of this conference will be held after the track and field events are completed. A shelter from the wind and rain will be located north of the tennis court, and an athlete registration area will be located south of the team ball court. To the west of the tennis and team ball courts and east of the straight track, a viewing shed will be built for important guests. Viewing platforms will be located to the north and south of the viewing shed. Viewing platforms will also be located to the north of the track and field area, outside the circular track, and to the east and west of the chairman's shed. Viewing platforms will also be located to the south and west of the circular track. The viewing platforms will be constructed of stone. The eastern viewing platform will have two sides, with a height of a dozen layers, and will be able to accommodate more than 30,000 people. Railings will be set up in front of the viewing platforms and inside the circular track. Only staff and athletes will be allowed to enter the field. Doors will be set up at appropriate locations in the railings to serve as entrances to the field. A total of six toilets will be set up throughout the field. A well will be opened in the original office building, and an additional office will be set up to the west. With this expansion and renovation, the field will be sufficient for the conference, and the road to Thousand Buddha Mountain will be to the west of the sports field, and the road to Kaiyuan Temple will be to the east. Provincial Chairman Han Fuqu ordered the Municipal Bureau of Public Works to build a flat road before the conference, which will further enhance the scenery.

Election Affairs Office of the People's Assembly Handles Election Preparation Schedule

▲ Citizens Should Understand Eighteen Key Points

The election affairs office for the People's Assembly representatives in this city has moved entirely into the Foreign Affairs Building since yesterday and is officially operating there. On Monday, Supervisor Zhang Qun convened the first office affairs meeting and resolved several important cases. The preparation schedule and election key points are listed below.

▲ National Assembly Representative Election Preparation Schedule March 2nd to 5th: (1) Internal Group; (2) Compile and print election laws and regulations and registration forms for various groups, which must be completed within the deadline; (3) Notify various groups to handle elections and come to the office within the 6th, 7th, and 8th to collect registration forms, and the deadline for submitting them in full is the 15th of this month. Late submissions will not be accepted. March 6th to 15th: (1) Distribute registration forms to various national organizations; (2) Ballot boxes, master registers of electors, registers of electors, voting books, and ballot papers will be issued separately, but the master registers of electors and voting books must be submitted successively from the 12th, with the deadline being the 15th; (3) Dispatch personnel to investigate and urge the collection of registration matters; (4) Compile and print election guidelines and other publications for distribution to electors and administrators; (5) Review and approve the election qualifications of various groups and members. March 16th to 25th: (1) Review and approve the qualifications of various groups and members and announce them successively; (2) Submit the registration books of various groups to the General Office; (3) Compile a general register of electors by occupation and registers of electors and voting books for each group; (4) Accept electors' declarations of errors and omissions. March 26th to April 5th: (1) Compile master registers of electors, etc. successively; (2) Select and announce the election venues and dates for various groups; (3) Appoint and report on the appointment of voting and ballot counting administrators and election supervisors; (4) Prepare and distribute the election supplies. April 6th to 16th: (1) Various groups hold elections separately; (2) Compile the number of votes for the elected and review their qualifications. April 17th to 26th: (1) Announce and notify the elected candidates; (2) Issue certificates of election; (3) Report on the completion of the election and the names of the elected candidates; (4) Handle various unfinished election matters. April 27th to 30th: (1) Handle the conclusion; (2) Transfer and custody.

▲ What Shanghai Citizens Should Know About the National Assembly "Why is the National Assembly convened this year?" The Fourth Plenary Session of the Third Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang was held from November 12th to 18th, 1930. During this meeting, it was decided to convene the National Assembly in the capital on May 5, 1931. Originally, the National Assembly was what the Premier hoped to see realized in the shortest possible time, but due to the successive disturbances and obstacles created by feudal warlords and other reactionary elements over the years, it has been delayed until now. If the Central Government had convened the National Assembly during that time of crisis, what would have been convened would have been a conference of warlords, politicians, and vagrants to divide the spoils, and it would certainly not have been the conference that the Premier wanted to convene and that the people hoped to see convened, a National Assembly in which the people could truly express their own opinions and views when the local areas were free from the oppression and coercion of the warlords. Therefore, the Central Government is only implementing the convening of the National Assembly this year, when the wars have been pacified and the country is in a stable state, which is truly in line with the Premier's legacy, which must be realized in the shortest possible time. "The significant difference between the National Assembly and the National Congress" Some people may not be very clear about the nature of the National Assembly and the National Congress and may easily misunderstand them. In fact, the National Assembly and the National Congress do have differences, the most significant of which are: 1. Different organizations; 2. Different powers. The organizational difference, first of all, in terms of organization, the National Assembly is organized by representatives of existing professional groups across the country, its content is determined by the Premier at that time as modern industrial groups, chambers of commerce, educational associations, universities, provincial student federations, labor unions, and farmers' associations, which together oppose Cao Wu's various armies, and political parties, while the National Congress is not. Article 14 of the Founding Outline states, "After the establishment of local autonomous governments in each county, one national representative shall be elected to form a representative assembly to participate in central political affairs." In this way, it is clear that the National Congress is organized by representatives elected by each autonomous county, which is very different from the organization of the National Assembly. The difference in powers, secondly, in terms of powers, the purpose of our party's advocacy of convening the National Assembly is to unify the minds and aspirations of the people across the country in order to seek the unification and construction of China, to solve the national livelihood problems internally, and to break the political and economic aggression of the great powers externally. This is just as the Premier said, "The destiny of the Republic of China lies in the self-determination of the people. If our party can obtain the assistance of the people, then the goals of China's independence, freedom, and unification will surely be achieved through struggle." Therefore, the National Assembly is a gathering to solve important issues in the current period of political tutelage. As for the National Congress, Article 23 of the Founding Outline states, "Then the National Congress shall be convened to determine the constitution and promulgate it." Article 24 also states, "Then the National Congress shall have the right to elect and recall officials of the central government, and shall have the right to initiate and veto central laws." According to this, the powers of the National Congress, in a negative sense, are to amend the constitution and laws and to punish government personnel for dereliction of duty. In other words, it is the highest authority for the people to exercise political power, which is significantly different from the National Assembly. "The important mission of the National Assembly" Since we have recognized the different characteristics of the National Assembly and the National Congress, we can now simply and affirmatively say that the National Congress is a gathering in a time of national prosperity, while the National Assembly is an important gathering to solve the life and death of the Chinese nation at present, and it is the only key to achieving peaceful unification and eternal freedom from war. The reason why China has not been able to unify and build in the past is really the result of the interaction between the people's suffering and the aggression of the great powers. We should take advantage of this unprecedented and unrepeatable National Assembly to gather the minds and aspirations of the people across the country and concentrate the abilities of the people across the country to make a proper solution in order to establish the foundation of a government of the people, by the people, and for the people, and to create a Republic of China based on the Three Principles of the People. All Chinese citizens should pay full attention to this. "Stipulating a Provisional Constitution" The previous paragraph was about the important mission of the National Assembly. In fact, during this grand meeting, we should also do the most important and urgent thing, which is to have all the representatives in the meeting establish a provisional constitution that the Chinese Kuomintang and the people of the whole country jointly abide by within the scope of the political tutelage of the Three Principles of the People, in order to establish a grand plan for long-term peace and stability. Because the meaning of the word "provisional" is originally "economy" and "restraint", now we sincerely hope that all the representatives in the meeting will earnestly study all the Premier's teachings, extract the clauses, and use them as a restraint between the government and the people in order to establish the foundation of a political system for all the people. This is something that must be especially emphasized. "Number of National Representatives" Now the National Assembly Representative Election Law and the National Assembly Representative Election Law Enforcement Law have been promulgated by the National Government one after another. The total number of National Assembly representatives is 520. "Number of Representatives from this City" This city should elect five representatives. "Groups that Produce Representatives" These five representatives are elected by (1) farmers' associations elect two representatives; (2) labor unions elect one representative; (3) chambers of commerce and industrial groups elect one representative; (4) educational associations, national universities, universities registered with the Ministry of Education, and freelance professional groups elect one representative; (5) the Chinese Kuomintang elects one representative. However, the farmers' associations, labor unions, chambers of commerce, educational associations, and other groups mentioned above are limited to those established in accordance with the law. As for industrial groups, they should also meet the following two conditions: (1) their members are indeed engaged in various industries with capital or skills; (2) they have been registered with the competent authorities. The freelance professional groups mentioned above include professional groups organized by news reporters, lawyers, doctors, engineers, and accountants who have been registered with the competent authorities. "Scope of Representative Production" Because the number of people in each group is very large, the scope of representative production has to be stipulated. In the farmers' association, the representatives should be elected by the members of the district farmers' associations in this city who attend the municipal farmers' association. In the labor union, the representatives should be elected by the members of the district labor unions in this city. As for the representatives of the chambers of commerce and industrial groups, they should be elected by the members of the same trade associations and stores in this city who attend the municipal chamber of commerce and the members of the industrial groups. Regarding the fourth article, the representatives of the educational association, national universities, universities registered with the Ministry of Education, and freelance professional groups should be elected by the members of the district educational associations in this city who attend the municipal educational association, and the current faculty and staff and undergraduate students in national universities registered with the Ministry of Education, and the members in freelance professional groups. In addition, one representative of the Chinese Kuomintang is elected by all the members in this city in the district branch when they hold a party member congress from among the candidates proposed by the central government. The above is the scope of representative production. We will explain the standards and qualifications of the elected candidates below. "Standards of Elected Candidates" Since we know that the mission of this National Assembly is very important, the representatives who attend this meeting should of course be very perfect people. Therefore, we should not elect those who (1) have committed counter-revolutionary acts that have been determined by a judgment or are still wanted; (2) have been found guilty of corruption while serving in public office; (3) have been deprived of their civil rights and have not yet been restored; (4) have mental illness or bad habits; (5) have been members of the Chinese Kuomintang and have been expelled from the party or had their party rights suspended. "Qualifications of Elected Candidates" Not only that, but even if a person does not have the bad behaviors mentioned above, we still cannot consider him to have the qualifications to serve as a representative of the National Assembly. For example, if a person has only two or three years of experience in the righteous business, he certainly cannot thoroughly understand the rural living conditions and the rural economic conditions. How can he represent the general farmers to attend the National Assembly? Therefore, the central government has also stipulated considerable restrictions on the qualifications of representatives. This restriction is that regardless of which sector the elected candidate is, they must have been engaged in the business of that sector for the following number of years and have not yet changed careers: (1) engaged in agriculture for more than ten years; (2) engaged in industry or commerce for more than five years; (3) engaged in education for more than five years; (4) engaged in various freelance professions for more than five years. "Content of Compiling Registers" Before holding the election, each group should first compile a register for Star News to review. The following should be stated in this register: (1) the organizational charter, establishment procedures, and process; (2) the registration authority and the date of registration; (3) the names and brief biographies of the staff; (4) the names, ages, birthplaces, addresses, and the number of years they have been engaged in the profession of the members; (5) if a member is also a member of another group, then the name of the other group and the group selected by the member should be stated. When compiling the register, people with the same surname should be combined and written together to facilitate review. "Announcement of the General Register of Electors" After the election supervisor in this city receives the aforementioned register, he will submit it for review. After the review is completed, he will compile the general register of electors and the register of electors for each group in this city by occupation and announce them on a regular basis. "Methods for Errors and Omissions" After the register is announced, if anyone believes that there are errors or omissions, they can obtain evidence and submit it to the election supervisor in this city for verification within five days. "Regulations for Withdrawing from the Election Venue" The venues and dates for the elections of various groups in this city are designated and announced by the election supervisor in this city. However, we should maintain order when we are in the election venue and do not make noise. If there are the following circumstances: (1) impersonation; (2) making noise in the venue, persuading others, and refusing to obey orders; (3) carrying weapons into the venue; (4) suspected of interfering with the election; (5) other improper behavior and refusing to obey orders, then the election personnel will order the elector to withdraw from the election venue. This is a very shameful thing. "Election Tickets are Completely Invalid" As for filling out the election tickets, you should be very careful, and the handwriting should be clear and not sloppy, because the Election Law Enforcement Law stipulates that all of the following are completely invalid: 1. those that are not written in the prescribed format; 2. those that have other characters written on them (but the addresses, occupations, and years of engagement in the occupation of the elected candidates are not subject to this restriction); 3. those that do not use the ballot paper issued. "Election Tickets are Completely Invalid or Partially Invalid" This is because, all of the following have the possibility of being completely invalid or partially invalid: 1. the handwriting is blurred and cannot be recognized; 2. the elected candidate is not in the general register of electors; 3. the occupation of the elected candidate does not belong to that sector. These must be paid special attention to. "Methods for Natural Disasters or Accidents" There is one more point that can be mentioned in passing, that is, if a natural disaster or other accident occurs in this city when handling the election, so that voting cannot be carried out, then the voting administrator can report to the election supervisor in this city and request a change in the voting date and voting venue. After the change, another announcement will be made. "The Election is Completed and the Ballots are Counted" We have voting administrators, ballot counting administrators, and election supervisors in the election venue. They are responsible for the various responsibilities of voting administration, ballot counting administration, and election supervision, respectively. After the voting is completed, the ballot counting administrator will start counting the ballots and continue until it is completed. "Notes for Elected Candidates" After the ballot counting is completed, those who receive the most votes are elected. If you are elected, the election supervisor in this city will give you a certificate of election. After you receive the certificate of election, you should indicate in writing within ten days that you are willing to be elected. If you do not indicate within the deadline, it will be considered that you are unwilling to be elected, and the person with the next highest number of votes will be substituted. If you are willing to be elected, then you should prepare all your luggage and quietly wait for the order of the National Government. This order is to notify you of the date to go to the capital. You should go to report within the deadline and verify your certificate of election. The above can be said to be a few common points of discussion regarding this election of National Assembly representatives. As for the details of each point, we would like to ask you to refer to the "Election Guide" published by this office.

Methods for Exemption of Customs Duties on Cotton Textiles Have Been Determined

▲ Exchange Yarn Tax Bills for Fabric Shipping Bills

The textile industry is exempt from customs duties when cotton yarn that has been subject to the consolidated tax is made into dyed and woven products for export. This has been clearly stated in the regulations for the collection of the consolidated tax on cotton yarn promulgated by the Ministry of Finance. However, because the implementation procedures have not yet been determined, customs duties are still being collected as usual. This has become an important issue for the textile industry. Yesterday, a reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency visited Mr. Zhu Wenqi, Chairman of the Mercerized Cotton Textile Industry Association, to inquire about the details. According to him, the industry has contacted the Consolidated Tax Office and the Jiangsu Consolidated Tax Bureau successively and has determined the following methods: All yarns that have been subject to the consolidated tax will not be subject to customs duties when they are made into woven products. However, when transporting and exporting, the yarn tax bills that have been subject to the consolidated tax must be submitted to the bureau in exchange for shipping bills, that is, the weight on the yarn tax bills will be used to offset the weight of the fabric (for example, each yarn tax bill is for 415 pounds of yarn, which can be exchanged for 415 pounds of fabric shipping bills). In order to facilitate the exchange of military supplies by various factories, the Consolidated Tax Bureau can send personnel to be stationed permanently in the Mercerized Cotton Textile Industry Association to handle this procedure. The above-mentioned methods have been submitted by the Jiangsu Consolidated Tax Bureau to the Consolidated Tax Bureau for approval and should be implemented in a few days.

After Customs Brokers Cease Reporting Cotton Yarn Shipments

▲The Yarn Manufacturers Association requests immediate compliance with reporting

▲Customs Brokers to hold a general meeting today to discuss the matter

The city's customs brokers, faced with increased complexities and the need to advance customs duties after cotton yarn and cloth factories paid consolidated taxes, have ceased copying the "black corner" permits from the Customs House. This cessation is to maintain their professional interests. They ceased reporting cotton cloth, yarn, and other goods from the first of this month and notified the Chinese Cotton Yarn Manufacturers Association and the Cotton Cloth Traders Association. Yesterday, the Chinese Cotton Yarn Manufacturers Association replied, stating: "Regarding your letter of February 28th, stating that despite the imposition of consolidated taxes on yarn and cloth, the Jianghai Customs still requires inspection and tax payment, causing significant advances in funds and burdensome procedures, a temporary general meeting resolved that as of March 1st, they will not be able to transport yarn and cloth without permits. After investigating, it was found that the Customs still collects taxes on yarn and cloth that have already paid consolidated taxes. The Association has repeatedly negotiated with the Consolidated Tax Office. According to their reply, the Customs' re-assessment of cotton yarn and cloth has been addressed by sending a letter to the Customs Administration to instruct the Customs to cease collection. The Director-General of Customs replied that this order was issued in mid-March and circulated to all customs offices on the 20th, stipulating that customs duties collected on cotton yarn and other goods after February 1st should be refunded upon presentation of consolidated tax certificates. Accordingly, all customs offices should comply with this order, and there should be no more instances of re-assessment obstructing transportation. As for the inspection issue, it is a necessary procedure for the Customs. It is indeed very cumbersome, time-consuming, and inconvenient. However, due to legal requirements, it is not possible to request exemption from inspection. Moreover, the Customs is still in the trial phase regarding cotton cloth and cotton yarn for which consolidated taxes have been collected. Even if we want to request accommodation, we must wait two months before we can calmly present the actual difficulties and seek their adoption. The Association is in the same position, with the same interests, and will assist in any way possible. Please urge your association to quickly discuss sending colleagues to resume transportation as soon as possible to avoid unnecessary significant losses to both parties. We are sending this message for your information." The Cotton Cloth Traders Association has also replied to the Association, requesting that it immediately resume reporting to avoid significant losses. After considering the situation, the Customs Brokers Association has decided to convene a general meeting of all members today to discuss the matter.

National Federation of Commerce Sends Telegram Organizing a Business Tax Research Committee

The National Federation of Commerce sent a telegram stating: To the Provincial Federations of Commerce of Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Sichuan, Fujian, Yunnan, Hebei, Henan, Shandong, Shanxi, Gansu, Rehe, Chahar, Fengtian, Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang Provinces; the Guangdong Merchant Organization Steering Committee; the General Chambers of Commerce of Guizhou, Shaanxi, Xinjiang, Qinghai, and Nanning; the Chambers of Commerce of Ningxia and Kangding Counties; and the Chambers of Commerce of Beijing, Nanjing, Qingdao, Shanghai, and Hankou: With the abolition of likin and the implementation of business taxes to compensate for the loss of likin revenue, the implementation has been carried out in order. However, the business tax collection regulations promulgated by the provincial governments may be inappropriate or flawed due to officials being unable to concurrently engage in commerce and therefore being unfamiliar with commercial situations. The tax rates and collection methods may be either too lenient or too harsh, resulting in many difficulties in implementation. Jiangsu Province has already initiated the process, with the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce convening all chambers of commerce in the province to discuss the classification of business taxes and tax rate issues, as well as to discuss the reorganization of the Provincial Federation of Commerce. With the implementation of the provincial business tax imminent, the classification of business taxes, tax rates, and collection methods should be studied by merchants in each province and presented to the respective provincial and municipal governments. This will hopefully ensure cooperation between officials and merchants and maximize the benefits of implementation. We are sending this telegram for your information, and we hope that each Federation of Commerce, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, General Chamber of Commerce in the provincial capital, and County Chamber of Commerce will immediately send a telegram convening all chambers of commerce in their respective provinces to send representatives to organize a Business Tax Research Committee. The Committee should appropriately devise methods, review the classification, tax rates, and methods, and submit them to the provincial and municipal governments for implementation, ensuring that the national treasury is enriched without exhausting the people and that the tax base is wealthy without imposing harsh rates. If the provincial and municipal governments do not adopt them, please have the respective Provincial Federations of Commerce and Municipal Chambers of Commerce telegram detailed information to this Federation. This Federation will immediately forward it to the Ministry of Finance to request approval for implementation and to discuss reorganization and the organization of the Provincial Federation of Commerce. We hope that the establishment will be completed within a limited time. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Commerce; Su Minsheng, Zhang Yuquan, Lu Guangji, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, Peng Chuli, Permanent Committee Members; Bowing respectfully.

Municipal Civil Training Association Reprimands the First District Agricultural Consolidation Association

Guomin She reports that the Municipal First District Agricultural Consolidation Association submitted a presentation to the Municipal Party Headquarters opposing the organizational law that uses the District Farmers Association as the basic organization and requesting the promulgation of the organizational system of the Municipal Farmers Association. A person in charge of the Civil Training Association of the Municipal Party Headquarters told a Guomin She reporter that the Association has not yet received the presentation. However, the Association believes that the proposal of the District Farmers Association to establish Township Farmers Associations under the District Farmers Associations is legally inconsistent and that the accusations of monopoly and control are absurd. Yesterday, a staff member was sent to the Association to reprimand them and will issue an order to severely reprimand them when the presentation arrives at the Association.

Jiang Dingwen Held a Funeral for His Ancestors in Shanghai Yesterday

▲Over a Thousand Important Figures from All Walks of Life Attended

Mr. Zilang, the respected father of the Ninth Division Commander Jiang Dingwen, passed away from illness in his native Zhuji on September 4th of last year. Soon after, Madam Yu, Jiang's stepmother, also passed away in her hometown on December 8th of the same year. At that time, Jiang was at the front participating in the anti-rebellion work and was deeply saddened by the news. Therefore, he specially established a funeral preparation office in Shanghai to hold a funeral for his ancestors. The hall was set up in the Xu Garden on Connaught Road. The Chengzhu ceremony was held the day before yesterday (3rd), and yesterday (4th), representatives of important figures from the Central Government and the National Government, representatives of various Party, government, military, and police agencies in the city, and well-known figures from the Shanghai business, industry, and academic circles, numbering about a thousand people, attended. There was heavy traffic in front of the Xu Garden, and the scene was extremely grand. The sacrificial banners and elegiac couplets were beautiful. The layout of the sacrificial hall was extremely solemn. After the representatives and guests offered their condolences, Jiang Dingwen personally returned the greetings one by one and provided vegetarian meals with utmost care. It is said that Jiang's family is a prominent clan in eastern Zhejiang, with a tradition of scholarship. When Jiang Dingwen was young, his father taught him the principles of filial piety, fraternity, loyalty, and righteousness as the foundation for life, as well as the world situation and the gains and losses of governance in ancient and modern times. He also repeatedly exhorted him to distinguish between right and wrong, understand obedience and rebellion, be public-spirited and forgetful of self, and be patriotic and forgetful of family. The achievements of Commander Jiang today are due to this excellent family education.

Anqing Steamboat Strike: Authorities Mediate

The entire workforce, led by Lu Shuangxi, Li Changsheng, etc., of the Anqing steamboat of the Taikoo Company, opposed the comprador Fan Chenghua's forced collection of meal money from the middle-cabin workers, resulting in a major labor strike. The Seamen's Union negotiated with the company without success and was forced to petition the Ministry of Industry for assistance. The Ministry has now notified the Municipal Government for verification. The details of the situation are recorded below.

▲Workers' Conditions: After learning that Zhu Shaobai had been detained by the police, all the workers were overly frightened and became mentally ill. They angrily sent the worker to Tongde Hospital for treatment. He has now been discharged from the hospital but has not fully recovered. They submitted four conditions to the company, requesting that the comprador comply: (1) Restore Zhu Shaobai's job; (2) Compensate Zhu Shaobai for medical expenses; (3) The comprador should voluntarily clear the case with the police; (4) Never force middle-cabin workers to pay meal money. The comprador insisted on refusing, and there was no way to resolve the matter. The Seamen's Union then petitioned the Ministry of Industry for assistance. Because the incident occurred in Shanghai, the Ministry immediately ordered the Municipal Government to handle it.

▲Comprador's Submission: After the incident, the comprador Fan Chenghua submitted a request to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to convene a mediation in order to prevent the strike from escalating. He stated that the tea room meal subsidy was the same on all Taikoo Company ships and was not something that Chenghua could change on his own. How could it be called extortion? Unexpectedly, the tea room foreman Zhu Shaobai asked to collect the meal subsidy every time the ship arrived. At first, he tried to negotiate, then he procrastinated, and finally, he refused to pay and even used harsh words and was about to use force. Chenghua is in his sixties and weak. How could he withstand this intimidation? For the sake of self-defense, he had to call the police for temporary custody to avoid harm. He was soon released on bail and there was no oppression. Therefore, he requested that the authorities thoroughly investigate and uphold justice and allow for prompt and public mediation.

▲Authorities' Mediation: After receiving the notification from the Ministry of Industry, the Municipal Government immediately sent staff to negotiate with the French police and learned that the worker Zhu Shaobai had been released. The police agreed to pay special attention to similar incidents in the future. Because the matter concerned labor disputes, the Municipal Government instructed the Social Affairs Bureau to verify the matter and handle it. At the same time, the Secretariat sent a letter to the Seamen's Union. After receiving the instructions from the Municipal Government, the Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhu Yuanlin to thoroughly investigate the matter in order to verify it.

Continued News of the Gonghe Case

Since the Seamen's Union took over the handling of the Gonghe Steamboat tea room dispute, Shen Huating has personally gone to Wuhu to surrender himself. The investigators sent to Wuhu by the Shanghai Seamen's Branch have returned to Shanghai and reported the truth to the General Union (the original report is very long, omitted). The murderers in this case are Hu Keming, Cheng Youbiao, Cao Wenzhi, Lao Chi, Song Weihua, Wan Xi, Jin Bangcai, and others, a total of nine people, who have been detained by the Wuhu Court. A notice was issued yesterday as follows: Notice regarding the fact that after the Dianan case on the Gonghe Steamboat occurred this year, it was rumored that Shen Huating had colluded with a number of illegal compradors and planned to use money to hire gangsters to disguise themselves as passengers on the ship, deliberately causing trouble in order to destroy the workers and disrupt the labor movement. After hearing this information, the Union believes that this conspiracy has a significant impact on the future of our seamen. Therefore, in addition to reporting the situation to the Central Government and the General Union for record, we hereby notify all workers to take note. In the future, all workers should treat people with courtesy and work carefully to show vigilance. This is important. This notice is issued on March 4, 2020, by He Zhenhuan, Lu Lezhi, and Tang Hesheng, Permanent Committee Members.

However, there are starving people everywhere here waiting to be fed. If the delay continues, more people will die. Please find a way to expedite the implementation so that spring relief can be organized in time. The barren fields can also be cultivated with the help of rain and snow. The people are waiting eagerly and urgently. Sand Fishing Boats Registered and Managed Like Cargo Ships

▲Abolish the Sand Fishing Name

▲Increase Cargo Ship Grades

Sand fishing boats entering and leaving the Wusongkou in the city were previously registered by the Municipal Port Affairs Bureau. There was a sand fishing boat registration office in Wusong. At the end of the 19th year, the Port Affairs Bureau was abolished, and the relevant affairs were transferred to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau. The Bureau then changed the sand fishing boat registration office to the Wu Port Shipping Office, and all sand fishing boats and cargo ships were registered, inspected, and issued licenses. Now, in order to classify sand fishing boats according to their nature as one of the types of cargo ships, the Municipal Government approved the abolition of the sand fishing boat name and managed them in the same way as other cargo ships in order to unify them. In addition, the cargo ships only have seven grades, but there are many sand fishing boats with an area above the seventh grade. The Finance Bureau also determined the grades of cargo ships and increased them to twelve. Generally, the eighth grade is for 100 square meters or more, and each additional 100 square meters increases by one grade, up to the twelfth grade for 500 square meters or more. It is reported that the registration of sand fishing boats according to cargo ships will soon be announced.
